comments</p> </a> </div> <!-- ad: https://mads.dailymail.co.uk/v6/us/news/none/article/other/para_top.html --><div class="adHolder column-content cleared"><div id="para_top" style="width:638px; margin:0 auto;"><script>var googletag = googletag || {};\ngoogletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];\n\ngoogletag.cmd.push(function() {\n    googletag\n        .defineSlot(\'/\' + .addService(googletag.pubads());\n        \n    googletag.display(\'para_top\');\n});</script></div></div> <p></p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">The head of the White House security office is seriously ill with <a style="font-weight: bold;" href="/news/coronavirus/index.html" id="mol-36ff8bb0-08fc-11eb-9a69-833556dd5753">COVID-19</a> and has been in hospital since September, according to reports.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Crede Bailey, who is in charge of issuing security credentials to the building and liaising with the Secret Service on the compound, fell ill before the September 26 Rose Garden \'super spreader event\', <a style="font-weight: bold;" class="class" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-10-07/white-house-security-official-contracted-covid-19-in-september?sref=yYYRek8e">Bloomberg</a> reported on Wednesday.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The White House has not disclosed Bailey\'s illness, which was confirmed to Bloomberg by four sources.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">On Wednesday night it was confirmed that the Marine Corps\' second-highest-ranking officer has tested positive.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Gen. Gary L. Thomas, the 58-year-old assistant commandant of the Marine Corps, had been in self-quarantine since Tuesday \'out of an abundance of caution\' after being notified he had recently been in contact with someone who later tested positive, a statement from the service said.\xc2\xa0</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">If Bailey\'s diagnosis is confirmed, it means that at least 34 people in <a style="font-weight: bold;" href="/news/donald_trump/index.html" id="mol-36f3a4d0-08fc-11eb-9a69-833556dd5753" class="class">Donald Trump</a>\'s orbit are now known to have become infected, according to a leaked FEMA tally.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group" style="style"> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-ee984be1c11d6d35" </div></div></div><mol-permabox id="mol-340493d0-08ff-11eb-be1a-09c452c870eb"><div class=" mol-factbox news art-ins" data-version="2" id="mol-1f1eed50-0646-11eb-ae3e-e3c873063f7e" data-permabox-url="/news/fb-8811661/TRUMPS-INNER-CIRCLE-TESTED-POSITIVE-COVID.html"><h3 class="mol-factbox-title">TRUMP\'S INNER CIRCLE WHO HAVE TESTED POSITIVE FOR COVID</h3><div class="ins cleared mol-factbox-body"><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font color="#000000"><b><u>WEDNESDAY OCTOBER 1</u></b></font></p><div class="mol-img-group float-r mol-hidden-caption" style=""> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-111895d2125196e0" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34013830-0-image-a-6_1602004186368.jpg" height="278" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" style="max-width:100%" /> </div> <noscript> <img id="i-111895d2125196e0" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34013830-0-image-a-6_1602004186368.jpg" height="278" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <p class="imageCaption"></p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">Ronna McDaniel, 47, Chair of the Republican National Convention</span>\xc2\xa0</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">McDaniel is thought to have been the first positive case. It was not made public until after Trump\'s diagnosis.\xc2\xa0</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">She was last in contact with Trump on September 25.\xc2\xa0McDaniel began isolating on September 26 when a member of her family tested positive. She got her results several days later.\xc2\xa0</p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold mol-style-underline">THURSDAY OCTOBER 2</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">Hope Hicks, 31,\xc2\xa0Counselor to the President</span></p><div class="mol-img-group float-r mol-hidden-caption" style=""> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-98610e48fcb342aa" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012094-0-image-a-1_1602004186352.jpg" height="306" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" style="max-width:100%" /> </div> <noscript> <img id="i-98610e48fcb342aa" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012094-0-image-a-1_1602004186352.jpg" height="306" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <div><div> <span></span> <div></div></div></div><p class="imageCaption">\xc2\xa0</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">Hicks was the first case reported and was tied to the President\'s positive test.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">She flew with him through the week before he was diagnosed and started feeling unwell on her way back from a rally in Minnesota on Wednesday night.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">She quarantined on Air Force One to stay away from him.\xc2\xa0\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">President Donald Trump, 74\xc2\xa0</span></p><div class="mol-img-group float-r mol-hidden-caption" style=""> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-98610c256d0342aa" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012094-0-image-a-2_1602004186353.jpg" height="280" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" style="max-width:100%" /> </div> <noscript> <img id="i-98610c256d0342aa" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012094-0-image-a-2_1602004186353.jpg" height="280" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <p class="imageCaption"></p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">Confirmed positive diagnosis on Friday October 2 at 1am. Was taken to Walter Reed on Friday night, where he remained on Monday afternoon.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">Reported symptoms included trouble breathing, lethargy and a fever.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">He was given an antibody cocktail on Friday and other treatments.\xc2\xa0</span></p><div class="mol-img-group float-r mol-hidden-caption" style=""> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-44e03023d3e194c4" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012172-0-image-a-7_1602004186369.jpg" height="290" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" style="max-width:100%" /> </div> <noscript> <img id="i-44e03023d3e194c4" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34012172-0-image-a-7_1602004186369.jpg" height="290" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <p class="imageCaption">\xc2\xa0</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">First Lady Melania Trump, 50</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">Confirmed positive diagnosis on Friday October 2 at 1am. She has been quarantining in the White House.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="">She suffered mild symptoms including a cough and a headache but has said repeatedly that she feels \'good\'.\xc2\xa0</span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold"><span class="mol-style-underline">FRIDAY OCTOBER 2</span></span></p><div class="mol-img-group float-r mol-hidden-caption" style=""> <div class="mol-img"> <div class="image-wrap"> <img id="i-beb4637a9bc19e65" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34014068-0-image-a-5_1602004186367.jpg" height="283" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" style="max-width:100%" /> </div> <noscript> <img id="i-beb4637a9bc19e65" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2020/10/06/18/34014068-0-image-a-5_1602004186367.jpg" height="283" width="284" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <p class="imageCaption"></p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">Fr.
